â”‚ Reduced motion handling: Currently each component checks prefers-reduced-motion in their useAnimation config. With CSS-only approach, use @media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) in CSS to set animation: none. This is actually better - declarative, no JavaScript overhead. Each component's CSS will have the @media query.   â”‚
